 If you have some questions related to this decision, then you will get answers here
 
 
 1
 Which part of the reservation will the upper castes get? The Modi government has promised to give 10 per cent reservation to the poor upper castes, this reservation will be different from the 50 per cent given till now
 yani, samvidhan ke anusaar abhi tak sirf 50 fisadi aarakshan diya jaataa he jo ki samaaj ke pichde tabake ko miltaa he
 That is, the government has given the decision to give reservation to the upper castes separately, for this the constitution will have to be amended
 2
 There is no provision in the constitution, how will it be found? Modi government will amend the constitution to implement this decision
 mangalvaar ko hi loksabhaa main samvidhan sanshodhit bill pesh kiya jayega

 The mathematics of net run rate has almost ended Pakistan's journey to this World Cup
 aaie samajhate hai net ran rate kii puri kahani
 Why the net run rate is needed? In a one-day tournament, the net run rate is required when two teams have equal points
 aisi sthiti main kisi ek team ke chayan ke liye yah ek saamaanya pranali hoti he
 The team which is on edge in net run rate goes ahead in the tournament
 net ran rate toornament ke us match ke nikaale jate hai, jiske rigelt aa chuke hai
 How the net run rate is calculated, divide the number of runs that the team has scored in the number of overs they have played
 ise aap aasaan shabdon main prati over ballebaaji kaa ausat bhi kah sakate hai
 Now take out how many runs scored per over against that team, that is, what the bowling average was
